<Text>There's a lot to be said about Florin Reservoir Park, and even more to be seen. The green lush grass is cut every week, there's also a fenced area with lights and a few metal benches for watching or playing soccer. I like to come here and enjoy my lunch break because sometimes there's massive games of rugby or soccer and you can watch for free! It's very entertaining and I would definitely recommend coming here for a birthday party or just to hang out. There is no bathroom at all and sometimes the parking is scarce due to residents nearby parking there. If your in Sacramento and you need a quick place to post up and relax this is one of those places. Thank you for reading this review and I hope it helped! Enjoy Florin Reservoir Park.</Text><pictures>None<//pictures>< date>

<Time>1554951492600<//Time><rating>5< /rating></record>
</dataset><record>
<user>102918253898437847981< /user><resp>None</resp><Review>Piadina - it's the bread!

Free sandwich with rewards registration/app download

Piadina reminds me of the build your own pizza places, such as Blaze & Mod Pizza.  GuestS can choose set sandwiches or make their own.  There is even a dough press, much like the pizza places.  Walking in, I was the only customer and asked for recommendations.

Having been told the 8)California was the most popular, with roasted chicken, mozzarella, arugula, tomatoes, avocado & basil pesto, I actually had it my way (since I wasn't feeling chicken) and ordered the 1)Parma, with prosciutto, mozzarella, mushrooms, arugula & tomatoes.

The piadina reminded me of naan, without the gluteny stretchiness.  Like scallion pancakes, without the grease.  The piadina was crispy, light & quite a pleasure to eat.  Decent portions of the proscuitto, I did find the Parma a little bland.  After a liberal dousing of balsamic vinegar and crushed red pepper, it became more towards my liking.

Service was good.  The parma was made in no time and I had my lunch ready.  Ample seating via booths, tables, both in & outdoors.  Parking is via  private lot.  Piadiana is located within a corporate park, surrounded by other eateries.

Piadina is one fine piece of bread.  I highly enjoyed the texture.  The establishment uses fresh, authentic ingredients & I didn't feel bloated and ready for a nap, afterwards.  Next time, methinks I'll go with the 6)Reggio, which is basically the 1)Parma, but kicked up a notch!  Can't wait!

Highly recommend!

<name>Thad King<//name><Date>1533057511245</Date><rating>2<//rating>< text>
I had seen commercials on television for Red Robin (Yum)  this particular Red Robin franchise was in the Thousand Oaks mall where parking is at a premium.   There is valet parking available for a 10 dollar fee. Back to Red Robin, the commercials showed a burger special with endless fries. The commercial made the burger special look spectacular and with endless fries how can you go wrong? We were seated quickly in the bar, the server behind the bar was quite personable and capable. He was quick to take our order and he delivered our drink order quickly. The delivery of the food seemed to take forever. When our food was delivered I was immediately disappointed. The burger's size more closely resembled a slider. My first bite of my meal was from the endless steak fries. Unfortunately the first fries were stone cold. My first bite of my burger was also stone cold. I imagine that the delay of our food was most likely due to our order sitting under the heat lamp. I imagined that the endless fries would come in a separate basket for our two orders. Instead they put the endless fries in the burger basket with a meager portion. I immediately ordered more fries and the bartender had the brilliant idea of ordering the fries with no salt so that they woukd come out hot and fresh. It worked! We sells ordered a hard cider on tap. The 22 oz. Pour was the best value and the cost was served in a short cold glass. That was our highlight of our experience.</text>

< text>
One of my favorite casual burger spots - great variety of burgers including price ranges, really good salads, sandwiches are great, and pretty good entr√©es. They are usually pretty crowded due to popularity so easier to just order take out - have been doing do for the past few years. Really good website ordering so you can customize to the Nth degree if you want. Relocated to a new area 4 mos ago and tonight was our 5th attempt at ordering to go. As usual, the website was perfect - it remembered our location of choice and was easy to log on to our loyalty account. As usual, finished the order and got the confirmation saying my order would be ready at 7:59pm. As usual,  I arrived on time to check in at the time the current confirmation told me to. As usual, the hostess told me they were working on my order. At 8:10pm I asked the hostess if she could check on my order since I could see a few to go orders being packed from where I was standing  and saw one of the bags get moved to a heat lamp. The hostess never came back. At 8:14pm a young man came to deliver a to go order but the customer had left for a moment. He saw me watching and asked if I was waiting for an order - I said yes and gave my wife's name- he said that my order was ready except for my drink (my order was the one on the heat lamp and had been there for about 5 min before I was told it was ready). He came back with my drink immediately and started to verify my order. I noticed there was no teriyaki sauce and no garlic bread - which is the norm for this location to forget. As he went to retrieve the missing items, I tasted one of the French fries and noticed that it was cold. Its 8:20 now and family expecting food so I didn't make the Temps an issue. Got home and salads on came with 1 mini cup of dressing and no breads sticks for the kids meal and the fruit was shabby at best. Been a fan for many years but this location is a no-go for me going forward. I hope this gets read by management there cause I can't get their attention while I'm in the restaurant.</text>

<Review>I should have checked the reviews before we entered this restaurant. They should fire the cook.

I remembered the great food and service in the Simi Valley location so I agreed to have lunch here.  Waiter service was ok. Food quality was very poor. I ordered 2 appetizers Voodoo fries and the Nachos.  The fries were supposed to have bacon & steak. The bacon could barely be detected and the steak was this funny looking breaded balls of something. The melted cheese was at the bottom of the fries, it had to be scraped with the fork to get a taste.  Finally the Nachos came after we were done with our small portion of fries.  The nachos were gross looking. Tortilla chips smothered in some type of dark brown ground beef chilly with black beans. Imagine a can of greasy chilly mix with another can of black beans. No salt.
A ball of what it appeared to be guacamole of to the side and 2 small containers, 1 with sliced whole jalapenos and the other with want to be salsa? pick de gallo?, it was sour so we really couldn't decide what it was.  It just set there in the middle of our table for the rest of the so called meal.

When I finally received the "Avocacobob" salad I ordered..it was a bigger disappointment. The lettuce was limp and darkened. Not crispy at all. The large amount of avocado slices in the picture of the menu consisred of these small chopped up in little squares that probably equaled the amount of 2 of the slices in the picture. The chicken was questionable between rubber and fake chiclen.

When the waiter finally came around  and asked how we were doing, I couldn't even look at him in the eye. I was embarrassed for them. Right before he came around to deliver our bill, be asked if we wanted more bottomless fries??...What???

I dont know why i asked him for a container for my untouched salad, it was just a waiste. I hate waiting food. He asked if we wanted a container for our Nachos to go and. We all said "No!", he laughed as he walked away.

Never Again.< /Review>< gmap_id>

<Review>It really hurts to finally write this review.  My family and I have been going to Emmy‚Äôs while they were still on Monterey Blvd when I was still a kid over 20 years ago!

However, Emmy‚Äôs has been declining specially the last three years.  The prices keep going up but the portions are smaller and the flavors are more bland perhaps to cater to the non-Asian customers.

I would order wor wonton soup, and they didn‚Äôt use to have bochoy in them so I was getting charged $1 extra to add them.  That was fine except they never put enough broth.  I was lucky to get even two tablespoons of broth!  I had to ask for more broth each time!  Finally, bochoy just became a staple of the wor wonton soup.  Today, the woman on the phone said she would add broth but she didn‚Äôt say she would charge me $3.50 for a tiny amount of broth that really should‚Äôve been part of the SOUP I ordered.  In other Asian restaurants, they put the soups in two containers to make sure there are plenty of broth and other ingredients.  I was also never charged by Emmy‚Äôs before for extra broth!

I used to order oysters with ginger & green onion but I stopped when they only put 3 oysters last time.  Two prior orders only had 4-5 oysters.  When I first ordered the dish there were always 6+.

The deep fried flounder that we used to order almost all the time was ordered less often the last six months.  The price kept getting higher but the fish kept getting smaller.

The very last time I ordered, I paid for two hot and sour soups but  they only delivered one.

Today was the final straw.  The woman was talking in Chinese to others while she was on the phone with me.  She also did not say I was getting charged for the extra broth.  When the driver called to clarify the price, she said she charged me $3.50 for the extra broth which I used to get for free.  My calculations also indicated, she actually charged me $5.  Then, I actually had to add salt and pepper just so I could taste something!  Bland, bland, bland!

Ma po tofu is supposed to be spicy!  Description even indicated spicy.  It was blander than bland.  My mom who thinks a little bit of pepper is spicy thinks this is bland! I had to add pepper and hot sauce!

The driver is an older gentleman who actually understands customer service when clearly his female boss does not.

In the last few years, I would order by calling them directly or used platforms like Eat24, Grub Hub, and Amazon when they have promotions.

20+ years of Emmy‚Äôs but higher prices, less portions, overcharges, no broth soups, bland foods, and management failures, I will have to order elsewhere.  I‚Äôve had better Chinese food in recent years but loyalty and the deep fried flounder were the only reasons I still ordered there.

<text>Decided to order delivery on a lark, and chose Emmy's. I ordered Vegetable Fried Rice, Chicken Chow Mein, and Beef and Broccoli. Ordering over the phone was okay- I had some difficulties understanding them but I wasn't certain whether it was the call quality or accent. The delivery time was as expected and the delivery man spoke English fluently and was perfectly polite. The food arrived hot. Overall service quality was Good.

As I ordered delivery, I did not visit the location, so I have marked it as Good to be neutral.

Unfortunately, the Fried Rice and Broccoli Beef were only fair, and the Chow Mein was down right bad, with unappetizing noodles and bland chicken. My assessment for food in this case is Poor-Fair.

Sadly, I won't be ordering from here again. The quality of the food is not worth the price.<//text>< Gmap_id>

< review>
At my house, every time we order Chinese food, its always Emmy's. It's always been Emmy's for as long as I could remember. Why? When there's a multitude of Chinese restaurants around our neighborhood like Yummy House and the once Hunan Nu-Lite Kitchen, now Beijing Restaurant, even the newly established Henry Hunan?! Why? Is a good question. I guess my family are just creatures of habit, it also helps that they're delivery is pretty quick.

Their menu is quite wide and varied enough to have something for everyone. I can't really attest to all of them, but I know for a fact for my personal taste buds that the chicken and BBQ pork chow mein, broccoli beef, BBQ pork fried rice, chow fun, Mongolian Beef, sweet and sour pork, Szechuan chicken, wonton soup, and their hot and sour soup are just absolutely delicious! For me personally, it's hard to compare their food from other places. I guess I just made them a standard since I've had their food for the longest time, really enjoying their preparation and flavor of their food.< /review>

< Text>
My sister is a huge fan of this place. She loves indian authentic food. Her office colleagues too have become addicted to the butter chicken,  saag paneer, the dum biryaniz from this place. I personally feel they have a great menu soc the top selling items , tandoor menu and the flavours are really very unique .
Veg platter, non  veg platter with salad its quiet filling. I feel rather than having a huge menu with chinese n other items and not delivering quality and taste, its better to have a menu one can cater with authentic taste, quality and consistency.  Their mutton biryani is way more better than any other restaurants i have tried till date. The fish tikka and chicken seekh kebab are worth ordering for parties and family occasions .
They had catered once for my sisters party and people loved the food. The pricing is very much cheaper compared to restaurants in mountain view area. This place is underrated i feel for the quality and tasteful food they cater. I would highly recommend this place and encourage people to write reviews which would help people rely on before they order.</Text>

I'm surprised by the way this restaurant has improved, compared to my previous visit, many months ago. I have noticed that they were getting many takeout orders.

I have ordered Hyderabadi chicken dum biryani. The service was on time. It took around 15 min for my order to arrive.
Biryani was very delicious. Perfectly cooked chicken, along with boiled egg, in a flavorful basmati rice. Gravy and raitha were also delicious..!!
Everything was so close to "authentic hyderabadi biryani" that I decided to write an updated review on yelp.

Only thing is, if they can improve the service in handling customers a little bit, this will be an awesome restaurant.

P.S. This review is only for the Hyderabadi chicken dum biryani. I will   definitely try other biryanis from this restaurant soon..!

Visit1
I decided to try this restaurant after seeing the name biryaniz and their tag line "asli biryani" (meaning original biryani). Went here for dinner on Tue.

Another crappy Indian restaurant just like many others in the south bay.
1) Unorganized. No one to seat you/ explain you/ to give the menu. You might feel other customers requesting you to move ( or touching) while eating because the tables are so close to each other that they can't leave until you move your chair forward.
2) Very slow. By the time you get your biryani your hunger will be dead. It took more than 30 min to get my order.
3) Bad service. Only 1 waiter trying to do everything. You have to keep asking the waiter again and again. Not just myself, there were other customers too requesting the waiter repeatedly that they didn't get their order served completely.
4) Flavorless Biryani. I still tried to be patient hoping the chicken dum biryani will be good but it is just bland biryani with too much rice and 2 chicken pieces and 1 egg.
mirchi ka saalan (gravy that comes with biryani) is all watery.
raita was ok.

P.S. This is Nakli biryani( meaning fake biryani). No way nearer to asli biryani as they claim. Another crappy biryani joint. Attached photos supporting my review.<//Review><user>113365907462512731207< /user></record></dataset><record>

<Rating>5<//Rating><Text>My husband and I walked into this restaurant on a whim with our 4 month old son. It was later at night and the staff greeted us with friendly smiles. They were running low on some of their staples but they eagerly talked us through the menu which helped us out a lot. I ordered a very spicy dish (I really like spicy food) and the man taking our order kindly let me know that their food is extra spicy compared to other local cuisines. He was right! I got the medium spice level and it was very spicy. I think they could tell I was having a bit of a tough time because they offered me extra raita sauce and a mango lassi. I couldn't believe how kind and friendly the service was. Not only that, but even though the dish was extremely spicy it was so delicious. It was worth every bite. I ordered a small and it was enough food for 3 meals and all for 14 dollars! The food was so fresh, and the service was above and beyond. Our 4 month old son started crying so we had to leave quickly after starting to eat, but the staff was super kind about it and gave us a carry out bag with extra sauces. I would say this is a great casual eating spot with incredible food and a relaxed family atmosphere. It was easy for us to wheel in our son's stroller. Their ordering process is very efficient too. You order at the register and they give you a number that you take to any table you want to sit at. Our food also came out relatively quickly. I'm so happy that this place is on Castro. It's a step above the other restaurants and half the price for the amount of food you get. I can't wait to go again!</Text>< pics>

<user_id>114714540192669718999< /user_id>< username>
B. Li< /username>
<time>1518499908405<//time>< Rating>
4</Rating>
< review>
Ordered the spicy shrimp biryani and fish biryani here.

The space is warm in feel and clean. Service is great, they really do go out of their way to ensure a welcoming experience.

The large portion of biryani truly is large; bring a second person or a big appetite. The basmati is light and fluffy, absorbs the yogurt and spicy flavors well. Do be warned that when you order spicy, it is indeed spicy. There is no playing around with the spices here. The flavors are intense and linger after the meal is over.

Between the fish and the shrimp, I'd recommend the fish. The meat and spicy sauce are at the base of the dish and it's up to the user's to make the rice as spicy as they'd like. This, however, means the protein can come out overcooked by the steam and heat. The shrimp can get a bit tough if you leave them there. The fish handles the heat much better.< /review>

<review>Biryaniz - Mountain View is the most authentic Biriyani place. Their Hyderabadi Goat Biryani and Lamb Keema Biryani are my favorite. Their biriyani's are delicious and authentic.
